country_event = { #ECW tree
	id = SCO.100
	title = SCO.100.t
	desc = SCO.100.desc

	picture = GFX_report_event_german_war

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event SCO.100"}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	option = {
		name =  SCO.100.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = liberal_democracy
				}
				load_focus_tree = { tree = SCO_ECW_tree keep_completed = yes }
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						has_government = social_democracy
					}
					load_focus_tree = {	tree = SCO_ILP_ECW_tree keep_completed = yes }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Collab Victory
	id = SCO.202
	title = SCO.202.t
	desc = SCO.202.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_edinburgh

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event SCO.202"}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = SCO.202.a
		SCO_Paranoia_Increase = yes
		SCO_Decrease_English_Approval_point_two = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = social_democracy
					has_government = liberal_democracy
				}
			}
			load_focus_tree = SCO_ENG_Victory_tree
		}

	}
}

country_event = { #HMMLR Victory
	id = SCO.203
	title = SCO.203.t
	desc = SCO.203.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_edinburgh

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event SCO.203"}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = SCO.203.a
		SCO_Paranoia_Decrease = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = liberal_democracy
			}
			load_focus_tree = SCO_FEN_Victory_tree
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = social_democracy
				}
				load_focus_tree = SCO_FEN_ILP_Victory_tree
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Germany vs Romania
	id = SCO.108
	title = SCO.108.t
	desc = SCO.108.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_german_war

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event SCO.108"}

	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = {check_variable = {
				SCOparanoia = 0
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			check_variable = {
				SCOparanoia = 10
			}
		}
		tag = SCO
		GER = {
			has_war_with = ROM

		}
	}



	option = {
		name = SCO.108.a
		SCO_Paranoia_Increase = yes
	}
}

###paranoia Idea Events

country_event = { #High Paranoia
	id = SCO.60
	title = SCO.60.t
	desc = SCO.60.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_scottish_soldiers
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event SCO.60"}

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_idea = SCO_Weapons_Free
		}
		tag = SCO
		check_variable = {
			SCOparanoia > 6
		}

	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = SCO.60.a
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = SCO_Itchy_Trigger
			add_idea = SCO_Weapons_Free
		}

	}
}

country_event = { #Medium Paranoia
	id = SCO.63
	title = SCO.63.t
	desc = SCO.63.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_scottish_soldiers
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event SCO.63"}

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_idea = SCO_Itchy_Trigger
		}
		tag = SCO
		check_variable = {
			SCOparanoia > 3
		}
		check_variable = {
			SCOparanoia < 7
		}

	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = SCO.63.a
		remove_ideas = SCO_Weapons_Free
		remove_ideas = SCO_Hands_Off
		add_ideas = SCO_Itchy_Trigger
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {SCOparanoia = 3}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {id = SCO.64 days = 20}
			}
		}
	}
}

###Oppression Idea Events

country_event = { #High Oppression
	id = SCO.80
	title = SCO.80.t
	desc = SCO.80.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_scottish_soldiers
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event SCO.80"}

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_idea = SCO_Very_Oppressive_State
		}
		tag = SCO
		check_variable = {
			SCOoppression > 14
		}

	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = SCO.80.a
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = SCO_Oppressive_State
			add_idea = SCO_Very_Oppressive_State
		}

	}
}

country_event = { #Medium Oppression
	id = SCO.81
	title = SCO.81.t
	desc = SCO.81.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_scottish_soldiers
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event SCO.81"}

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_idea = SCO_Oppressive_State
		}
		tag = SCO
		check_variable = {
			SCOoppression > 8
		}
		check_variable = {
			SCOoppression < 14
		}

	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = SCO.81.a
		remove_ideas = SCO_Very_Oppressive_State
		remove_ideas = SCO_Slightly_Oppressive_State
		add_ideas = SCO_Oppressive_State
	}
}

country_event = { #ECW tanks hmmlr
	id = SCO.225
	title = SCO.225.t
	desc = SCO.225.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_OST_tank

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event SCO.225"}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {

		name =  SCO.225.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dlc = "No Step Back"
			}
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = MBT_chassis
				amount = -40
				producer = SCO
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = MBT_equipment
				amount = -40
				producer = SCO
			}
		}
		FEN =  {
			country_event = {
				id = SCO.226
				days = 7
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #normal retirement triggered by victory foci
	id = SCO.303
	title = SCO.303.t
	desc = SCO.303.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_sco_flag

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event SCO.303"}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {

		name =  SCO.303.a
		country_event = {
			id = SCO.2
		}
		remove_unit_leader = 675
	}
}

country_event = { #vote
	id = SCO.302
	title = SCO.302.t
	desc = SCO.302.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_edinburgh

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event SCO.302"}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {#Young

		name =  SCO.302.a

		add_to_variable = {
			var = SCOsuccessor	value = 1
		}
		SCO_Paranoia_Decrease = yes
		SCO_Happiness_Decrease = yes
	}

	option = {#boswell

		name =  SCO.302.b

		SCO_Paranoia_Increase = yes
		SCO_Happiness_Increase = yes
		add_to_variable = {
			var = SCOsuccessor	value = 2
		}

	}

	option = {#Kennedy

		name =  SCO.302.c

		SCO_Paranoia_Decrease = yes
		add_to_variable = {
			var = SCOsuccessor	value = 3
		}
	}

	option = {#Miller

		name =  SCO.302.d

		add_to_variable = {
			var = SCOsuccessor	value = 4
		}
		SCO_Paranoia_Increase = yes

	}

}

country_event = { #coup event
	id = SCO.1000
	title = SCO.1000.t
	desc = SCO.1000.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_riot_police

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event SCO.1000"}


	fire_only_once = yes
	trigger ={
		tag = SCO
		AND = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = SCO_Coup_Disabled
					has_country_flag = SCO_Paranoia_Removed
				}
			}
			check_variable = {
				SCOparanoia > 7
			}
			check_variable = {
				SCOhappiness < 7
			}
		}

	}

	option = {
		name = SCO.1000.b
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				country_event = {
					id = WORLD.1993
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = 8_SCO_tt
		kill_country_leader = yes
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = despotism
			long_name = SCO_Armed_Forces_coup_long
			name = SCO_Armed_Forces_coup
		}
		set_country_flag = SCO_Military_Coup
		add_manpower = -1000
		add_stability = -0.3
		complete_national_focus = SCO_Coup
		set_variable = {
			var = SCOoppression
			value = 10
		}
		set_politics = { ruling_party = despotism }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable ={
					SCOsuccessor = 0
				}
			}
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = SCO_Douglas_Wimberley
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					desc = "POLITICS_DOUGLAS_WIMBERLEY_DESC"
					ideology = despotism_military_junta_subtype
					expire = "1990.1.1"
					traits = {
						Paranoid
					}
					id = -1
				}
			}
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = SCO_Bernard_Charles_Gordon_Lennox_hog
			add_ideas = SCO_Eric_Brown_for
			add_ideas = SCO_John_Gilmour_eco
			add_ideas = SCO_Alexander_Boswell_sec
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable ={
					SCOsuccessor = 1
				}
			}
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = SCO_Bernard_Charles_Gordon_Lennox
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					desc = ""
					expire = "1990.1.1"
					ideology = despotism_military_junta_subtype
					traits = {  }
					id = -1
				}
			}
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = SCO_Edmund_Walter_Anstice_hog
			add_ideas = SCO_Eric_Brown_for
			add_ideas = SCO_John_Gilmour_eco
			add_ideas = SCO_Alexander_Boswell_sec
		}


		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable ={
					SCOsuccessor = 2
				}
			}
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = SCO_Alexander_Boswell
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					desc = "POLITICS_ALEXANDER_BOSWELL_DESC"
					expire = "1990.1.1"
					ideology = despotism_military_junta_subtype
					traits = { Paranoid }
					id = -1
				}
			}
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = SCO_Winnie_Ewing_hog
			add_ideas = SCO_Douglas_Henderson_for
			add_ideas = SCO_Alexander_Cairncross_eco
			add_ideas = SCO_Ian_Oliver_sec
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable ={
					SCOsuccessor = 3
				}
			}
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = SCO_Eric_Brown
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					desc = ""
					expire = "1990.1.1"
					ideology = despotism_military_junta_subtype
					traits = {  }
					id = -1
				}
			}
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = SCO_Douglas_Crawford_hog
			add_ideas = SCO_Andrew_Gilchrist_for
			add_ideas = SCO_Alexander_Cairncross_eco
			add_ideas = SCO_Charles_Shaw_sec
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable ={
					SCOsuccessor = 4
				}
			}
			add_country_leader_role = {
				character = SCO_Edmund_Walter_Anstice
				promote_leader = yes
				country_leader = {
					desc = ""
					expire = "1990.1.1"
					ideology = despotism_military_junta_subtype
					traits = {  }
					id = -1
				}
			}
			add_ideas = SCO_Francis_McFadzean_hog
			add_ideas = SCO_Arnold_Clark_for
			add_ideas = SCO_Iain_Maxwell_Stewart_eco
			add_ideas = SCO_Alexander_Boswell_sec
		}

		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = despotism
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = despotism
			popularity = 0.74
		}
		load_focus_tree = { tree = SCO_Coup keep_completed = yes }
		ENG = {
			country_event = {
				id = SCO.306
				days = 10
			}
		}
		IRE = {
			country_event = {
				id = SCO.306
				days = 10
			}
		}
		ULS = {
			country_event = {
				id = SCO.306
				days = 10
			}
		}
		WAL = {
			country_event = {
				id = SCO.306
				days = 10
			}
		}


	}
}

	id = SCO.306
	title = SCO.306.t
	desc = SCO.306.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_riot_police

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event SCO.306"}


	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = SCO.306.a

	}
}

country_event = { #torture
	id = SCO.2003
	title = SCO.2003.t
	desc = SCO.2003.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_Welsh_Police
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event SCO.2003"}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = SCO.2003.a
		add_to_variable = {
			SCOoppression = 1
		}
		add_war_support = -0.05
		add_stability = 0.05
		custom_effect_tooltip = 3_SCO_tt
	}

	option = {
		name = SCO.2003.b
		add_war_support = 0.05
	}
}

country_event = { #Border
	id = SCO.2004
	title = SCO.2004.t
	desc = SCO.2004.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_Welsh_Police

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event SCO.2004"}


	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = SCO.2004.a
		add_to_variable = {
			SCOoppression = 1
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		add_war_support = -0.08
		custom_effect_tooltip = 3_SCO_tt
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = tno_immigration_quota_immigration
			add_idea = tno_immigration_closed_borders
		}
		TNO_improve_immigration_policy_effectiveness_monthly_low = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = SCO.2004.b
		add_stability = -0.12

	}
}

country_event = { #Press
	id = SCO.2005
	title = SCO.2005.t
	desc = SCO.2005.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_newspaper

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event SCO.2005"}


	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = SCO.2005.a
		add_to_variable = {
			SCOoppression = 1
		}
		add_political_power = 100
		add_war_support = 0.05
		add_stability = -0.1
		custom_effect_tooltip = 3_SCO_tt
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = tno_press_rights_free_press
			add_idea = tno_press_rights_state_press_only
		}
		TNO_improve_press_rights_policy_effectiveness_monthly_low = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = SCO.2005.b
		add_war_support = -0.1
		add_political_power = -40
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = tno_press_rights_free_press
			add_idea = tno_press_rights_censored_press
		}
		TNO_improve_press_rights_policy_effectiveness_monthly_low = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #politicians
	id = SCO.2006

country_event = { #1962 Election
	id = SCO.2712
	title = SCO.2712.t
	desc = SCO.2712.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_edinburgh

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event SCO.2712"}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = SCO.2712.a
		clr_country_flag = SCO_Election_Campaign_On
		clr_country_flag = SCO_Election_Campaign_1962
		clr_country_flag = president_campaign_already_done
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						check_variable = {
							SCO_Election_National_SNP_Percentage > SCO_Election_National_ILP_Percentage
						}
						check_variable = {
							SCO_Election_National_SNP_Percentage > SCO_Election_National_UP_Percentage
						}
						NOT = { 
							OR = {
								has_game_rule = { 
									rule = SCO_ELECTIONS_1962 option = SCO_ELECTIONS_1962_SNP
								}
								has_game_rule = { 
									rule = SCO_ELECTIONS_1962 option = SCO_ELECTIONS_1962_ILP
								}
								has_game_rule = { 
									rule = SCO_ELECTIONS_1962 option = SCO_ELECTIONS_1962_UP
								}
							}	
						}
					}

				}
				country_event = { id = SCO.2713 days = 2 }
			}
				
				


			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						check_variable = {
							SCO_Election_National_ILP_Percentage > SCO_Election_National_SNP_Percentage
						}
						check_variable = {
							SCO_Election_National_ILP_Percentage > SCO_Election_National_UP_Percentage
						}
						NOT = { 
							OR = {
								has_game_rule = { 
									rule = SCO_ELECTIONS_1962 option = SCO_ELECTIONS_1962_SNP
								}
								has_game_rule = { 
									rule = SCO_ELECTIONS_1962 option = SCO_ELECTIONS_1962_ILP
								}
								has_game_rule = { 
									rule = SCO_ELECTIONS_1962 option = SCO_ELECTIONS_1962_UP
								}
							}	
						}
					}

				}
				country_event = { id = SCO.2714 days = 2 }
			}

			
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						check_variable = {
							SCO_Election_National_UP_Percentage > SCO_Election_National_ILP_Percentage
						}
						check_variable = {
							SCO_Election_National_UP_Percentage > SCO_Election_National_SNP_Percentage
						}
						NOT = { 
							OR = {
								has_game_rule = { 
									rule = SCO_ELECTIONS_1962 option = SCO_ELECTIONS_1962_SNP
								}
								has_game_rule = { 
									rule = SCO_ELECTIONS_1962 option = SCO_ELECTIONS_1962_ILP
								}
								has_game_rule = { 
									rule = SCO_ELECTIONS_1962 option = SCO_ELECTIONS_1962_UP
								}
							}	
						}
					}

				}
				country_event = { id = SCO.2718 days = 2 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = { 
						rule = SCO_ELECTIONS_1962 option = SCO_ELECTIONS_1962_SNP 
					}	
				}
				country_event = { id = SCO.2713 days = 2 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = { 
						rule = SCO_ELECTIONS_1962 option = SCO_ELECTIONS_1962_ILP 
					}	
				}
				country_event = { id = SCO.2714 days = 2 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = { 
						rule = SCO_ELECTIONS_1962 option = SCO_ELECTIONS_1962_UP 
					}

			}

	}

country_event = { # 1966 Election Results
	id = sco_fen.78
	title = sco_fen.78.t
	desc = sco_fen.78.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_scottish_soldiers

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sco_fen.78"}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = sco_fen.78.a
		clr_country_flag = SCO_Election_Campaign_On
		clr_country_flag = SCO_Election_Campaign_1966
		clr_country_flag = president_campaign_already_done

		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						check_variable = {
							SCO_Election_National_SNP_Percentage > SCO_Election_National_ILP_Percentage
						}
						check_variable = {
							SCO_Election_National_SNP_Percentage > SCO_Election_National_UP_Percentage
						}
						NOT = { 
							OR = {
								has_game_rule = { 
									rule = SCO_ELECTIONS_1966 option = SCO_ELECTIONS_1966_SNP
								}
								has_game_rule = { 
									rule = SCO_ELECTIONS_1966 option = SCO_ELECTIONS_1966_ILP
								}
								has_game_rule = { 
									rule = SCO_ELECTIONS_1966 option = SCO_ELECTIONS_1966_UP
								}
							}	
						}
					}

				}
				country_event =  { #SNP
					id = sco_fen.79
					days = 5
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						check_variable = {
							SCO_Election_National_UP_Percentage > SCO_Election_National_ILP_Percentage
						}
						check_variable = {
							SCO_Election_National_UP_Percentage > SCO_Election_National_SNP_Percentage
						}
						NOT = { 
							OR = {
								has_game_rule = { 
									rule = SCO_ELECTIONS_1966 option = SCO_ELECTIONS_1966_SNP
								}
								has_game_rule = { 
									rule = SCO_ELECTIONS_1966 option = SCO_ELECTIONS_1966_ILP
								}
								has_game_rule = { 
									rule = SCO_ELECTIONS_1966 option = SCO_ELECTIONS_1966_UP
								}
							}	
						}
					}

				}
				country_event =  { #UP
					id = sco_fen.81
					days = 5

				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						check_variable = {
							SCO_Election_National_ILP_Percentage > SCO_Election_National_UP_Percentage
						}
						check_variable = {
							SCO_Election_National_ILP_Percentage > SCO_Election_National_SNP_Percentage
						}
						NOT = { 
							OR = {
								has_game_rule = { 
									rule = SCO_ELECTIONS_1966 option = SCO_ELECTIONS_1966_SNP
								}
								has_game_rule = { 
									rule = SCO_ELECTIONS_1966 option = SCO_ELECTIONS_1966_ILP
								}
								has_game_rule = { 
									rule = SCO_ELECTIONS_1966 option = SCO_ELECTIONS_1966_UP
								}
							}	
						}
					}

				}
				country_event =  { #ILP
				id = sco_fen.801
				days = 5
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = { 
						rule = SCO_ELECTIONS_1966 option = SCO_ELECTIONS_1966_SNP 
					}	
				}
				country_event = { id = sco_fen.79 days = 5 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = { 
						rule = SCO_ELECTIONS_1966 option = SCO_ELECTIONS_1966_ILP 
					}	
				}
				country_event = { id = sco_fen.801 days = 5 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_game_rule = { 
						rule = SCO_ELECTIONS_1966 option = SCO_ELECTIONS_1966_UP 
					}	
				}
				country_event = { id = sco_fen.81 days = 5 }
			}

		}
	}

}


country_event = { #SNP Victory 1966
	id = sco_fen.79
	title = sco_fen.79.t
	desc = sco_fen.79.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_scottish_soldiers

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sco_fen.79"}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = sco_fen.79.a
		hidden_effect = {
			add_stability = -0.1
			add_war_support = -0.1
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = liberal_democracy
			elections_allowed = no
		}


		hidden_effect = {
			remove_all_ministers = yes
			add_ideas = SCO_Arthur_Donaldson_hog
			add_ideas = SCO_George_Leslie_eco
			add_ideas = SCO_Iain_Maccormick_for
			add_ideas = SCO_Jimmy_Halliday_sec
			if = {
				limit = {has_country_flag = SCO_SNP_Detente }
				#load_focus_tree = SCO_1966_SNP_Detente_Victory
				set_popularities = {
					communist = 0
					ultranationalism = 0
					socialist = 0
					social_democracy = 30
					liberal_democracy = 56

					conservative_democracy = 14
					authoritarian_democracy = 0
					despotism = 0
					fascism = 0
					
				}
				else = {
					#load_focus_tree = SCO_1966_SNP_Victory
					set_popularities = {
						communist = 0
						ultranationalism = 0
						socialist = 0
						social_democracy = 30
						liberal_democracy = 60

						conservative_democracy = 10
						authoritarian_democracy = 0
						despotism = 0
						fascism = 0
						
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #random popularity (i pray this works)
	id = sco_snp.25
	title = sco_snp.25.t
	desc = sco_snp.25.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_edinburgh

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event SCO.100"}

	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes


	option = {
		name = sco_snp.25.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = {
						SCO_UK_Support > 0

					}
					check_variable = {
						SCO_UK_Support < 25

					}
					OR = {
						country_exists = FEN
						ENG = {
							has_country_leader = {character = ENG_Harold_MacMillan}
						}
					}

					NOT = {
						has_global_flag =  eng_burgundian_aid
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {has_government = liberal_democracy	}
				random_list = {
					30 = {
						subtract_from_variable = {
							SCO_UK_Support = 1
						}
					}
					30 = {
						add_to_variable = {
							SCO_UK_Support = 1
						}
					}
					40 = {

					}
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {has_government = conservative_democracy	}
				random_list = {
					20 = {
						subtract_from_variable = {
							SCO_UK_Support = 1
						}
					}
					40 = {
						add_to_variable = {
							SCO_UK_Support = 1
						}
					}
					40 = {

					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						has_government = social_democracy
						has_country_flag = SCO_ILP_Unionists
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					20 = {
						subtract_from_variable = {
							SCO_UK_Support = 1
						}
					}
					30 = {
						add_to_variable = {
							SCO_UK_Support = 1
						}
					}
					50 = {

					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					AND = {
						has_government = social_democracy
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = SCO_ILP_Unionists
						}
					}
				}
				random_list = {
					30 = {
						subtract_from_variable = {
							SCO_UK_Support = 1
						}
					}
					30 = {
						add_to_variable = {
							SCO_UK_Support = 1
						}
					}
					40 = {

					}
				}
			}

		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_war_with = FEN
					has_war_with = ENG
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = sco_snp.25
				days = 109 #should be 109
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					SCO_UK_Support = 0

				}
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				SCO_UK_Support = 1
			}

		}

	}

}

				long_name = SCO_authoritarian_democracy_UK_FEN_ILP_long
				name = SCO_authoritarian_democracy_UK_FEN_ILP
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {has_government = liberal_democracy	}
			set_popularities = {
				communist = 2
				ultranationalism = 0
				socialist = 8
				social_democracy = 21
				liberal_democracy = 31

				conservative_democracy = 29
				authoritarian_democracy = 9
				despotism = 0
				fascism = 0
				
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = liberal_democracy
				long_name = SCO_liberal_democracy_UK_FEN_SNP_long
				name = SCO_liberal_democracy_UK_FEN_SNP
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_democracy
				long_name = SCO_social_democracy_UK_FEN_SNP_long
				name = SCO_social_democracy_UK_FEN_SNP
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = conservative_democracy
				long_name = SCO_conservative_democracy_UK_FEN_SNP_long
				name = SCO_conservative_democracy_UK_FEN_SNP
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = socialist
				long_name = SCO_socialist_UK_FEN_SNP_long
				name = SCO_socialist_UK_FEN_SNP
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = communist
				long_name = SCO_communist_UK_FEN_SNP_long
				name = SCO_communist_UK_FEN_SNP
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democracy
				long_name = SCO_authoritarian_democracy_UK_FEN_SNP_long
				name = SCO_authoritarian_democracy_UK_FEN_SNP
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {has_government = conservative_democracy	}
			set_popularities = {
				communist = 2
				ultranationalism = 0
				socialist = 8
				social_democracy = 21
				liberal_democracy = 25

				conservative_democracy = 35
				authoritarian_democracy = 9
				despotism = 0
				fascism = 0
				
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = liberal_democracy
				long_name = SCO_liberal_democracy_UK_FEN_SNP_long
				name = SCO_liberal_democracy_UK_FEN_SNP
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_democracy
				long_name = SCO_social_democracy_UK_FEN_SNP_long
				name = SCO_social_democracy_UK_FEN_SNP
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = conservative_democracy
				long_name = SCO_conservative_democracy_UK_FEN_SNP_long
				name = SCO_conservative_democracy_UK_FEN_SNP

					#load_focus_tree = SCO_ILP_1970
					set_country_flag = SCO_ILP_1970_NOT_UNIONIST
					set_popularities = {
						communist = 0
						ultranationalism = 0
						socialist = 0
						social_democracy = 54
						liberal_democracy = 30

						conservative_democracy = 16
						authoritarian_democracy = 0
						despotism = 0
						fascism = 0
						
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	title = sco_collab.2087.t

	desc = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = USA
				tag = SCO
			}
		}
		text = sco_collab.2087.desc
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				tag = GER
				tag = ENG
			}
		}
		text = sco_collab.2187.desc
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_scottish_soldiers
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sco_collab.2087"}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = { #commit (WAR)
		name = sco_collab.2087.a
		trigger = {
			tag = USA
		}
		SCO = {
			country_event = {
				id = sco_collab.2089
				days = 1
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				country_event = {
					id = WORLD.2018
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #pul out
		name = sco_collab.2087.b
		trigger = {
			tag = USA
		}
		USA_decrease_ruling_party_popularity_2 = yes
		SCO = {
			leave_faction = yes
			country_event = {
				id = sco_collab.2077
				days = 2
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				country_event = {
					id = WORLD.2016
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = sco_collab.2087.c
		trigger = {
			tag = USA
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = sco_collab.2087.e
		trigger = {
			tag = SCO
			tag = ENG
		}
	}
}




















country_event = { #German Forces Attack (ENG)
	id = sco_collab.2088
	title = sco_collab.2088.t
	desc = sco_collab.2088.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_scottish_soldiers

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sco_collab.2088"}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = sco_collab.2088.a
		declare_war_on = {
			target = SCO
			type = annex_everything
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			USA = {
				country_event = {
					id = nuclearwar.4
					days = 6
				}
			}
		}


	}
}

country_event = { #hidden 1965 presidential election event
	id = SCO.40101
	title = SCO.40101.t
	desc = SCO.40101.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_scottish_soldiers

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event SCO.40101"}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	hidden = yes

	option = {
		name = SCO.40101.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = despotism
				}
				tag = SCO
			}
			country_event = {
				id = SCO.4010
			}
		}

	}
}



country_event = { #Presidential Election 1965 start
	id = SCO.4010
	title = SCO.4010.t
	desc = SCO.4010.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_scottish_soldiers

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event SCO.4010" }

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = SCO.4010.a
		SCO_Get_Percentage_of_Vote_Highlands = yes
		SCO_Get_Percentage_of_Vote_Aberdeenshire = yes
		SCO_Get_Percentage_of_Vote_Lanark = yes
		SCO_Get_Percentage_of_Vote_Fife = yes
		SCO_Get_Percentage_of_Vote_Dumfries = yes
		SCO_Get_Percentage_of_Vote_Lothian = yes
		SCO_Get_Percentage_of_Vote_National = yes
		SCO_Get_Turnout_National = yes

		set_country_flag = SCO_Election_Campaign_Presidential_1965
		set_country_flag = SCO_Election_Campaign_On
		set_country_flag = SCO_SNP_Campaign
		add_political_power = 20
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = SCO.7008
				days = 3
			}
			country_event = {
				id = SCO.7009
				days = 6
			}
		}

	}

	option = {
		name = SCO.4010.b
		SCO_Get_Percentage_of_Vote_Highlands = yes
		SCO_Get_Percentage_of_Vote_Aberdeenshire = yes
		SCO_Get_Percentage_of_Vote_Lanark = yes
		SCO_Get_Percentage_of_Vote_Fife = yes
		SCO_Get_Percentage_of_Vote_Dumfries = yes
		SCO_Get_Percentage_of_Vote_Lothian = yes
		SCO_Get_Percentage_of_Vote_National = yes
		SCO_Get_Turnout_National = yes

		set_country_flag = SCO_Election_Campaign_Presidential_1965
		set_country_flag = SCO_Election_Campaign_On
		set_country_flag = SCO_ILP_Campaign
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = SCO.7007
				days = 3
			}
			country_event = {
				id = SCO.7009
				days = 6
			}
		}

	}

	option = {
		name = SCO.4010.c
		SCO_Get_Percentage_of_Vote_Highlands = yes
		SCO_Get_Percentage_of_Vote_Aberdeenshire = yes
		SCO_Get_Percentage_of_Vote_Lanark = yes
		SCO_Get_Percentage_of_Vote_Fife = yes
		SCO_Get_Percentage_of_Vote_Dumfries = yes
		SCO_Get_Percentage_of_Vote_Lothian = yes
		SCO_Get_Percentage_of_Vote_National = yes
		SCO_Get_Turnout_National = yes

		set_country_flag = SCO_Election_Campaign_Presidential_1965
		set_country_flag = SCO_Election_Campaign_On
		set_country_flag = SCO_UP_Campaign
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = SCO.7008
				days = 3
			}

				days = 6

country_event = { #Presidential Election 1965 day
	id = SCO.4011
	title = SCO.4011.t
	desc = SCO.4011.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_scottish_soldiers

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sco_up_countercoup.3" }

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = SCO.4011.a
		clr_country_flag = SCO_SNP_President
		clr_country_flag = SCO_ILP_President
		clr_country_flag = SCO_UP_President
		clr_country_flag = SCO_Election_Campaign_On
		clr_country_flag = SCO_Election_Campaign_Presidential_1965
		clr_country_flag = president_campaign_already_done

		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = {
						SCO_Election_National_SNP_Percentage > SCO_Election_National_ILP_Percentage
					}
					check_variable = {
						SCO_Election_National_SNP_Percentage > SCO_Election_National_UP_Percentage
					}
				}

			}
			country_event = { id = SCO.4012 days = 2 }
		}




		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = {
						SCO_Election_National_ILP_Percentage > SCO_Election_National_SNP_Percentage
					}
					check_variable = {
						SCO_Election_National_ILP_Percentage > SCO_Election_National_UP_Percentage
					}
				}

			}
			country_event = { id = SCO.4013 days = 2 }
		}


		if = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = {
						SCO_Election_National_UP_Percentage > SCO_Election_National_ILP_Percentage
					}
					check_variable = {
						SCO_Election_National_UP_Percentage > SCO_Election_National_SNP_Percentage
					}
				}

			}
			country_event = { id = SCO.4014 days = 2 }
		}


	}
}

country_event = { #Presidential Election 1965 SNP Win
	id = SCO.4012
	title = SCO.4012.t
	desc = SCO.4012.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_edinburgh

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event sco_up_countercoup.3" }

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = SCO.4012.a
		set_country_flag = SCO_SNP_President
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = liberal_democracy
			}
			add_stability = 0.03
			add_political_power = 40
			else = {
				add_political_power = -50
			}
		}

	}
}

country_event = { #Scotland SNP AI Campaign
	id = SCO.7007
	title = SCO.7007.t
	desc = SCO.7007.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_scottish_soldiers

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event SCO.7006" }

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #SNP Campaign
		name = SCO.7007.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = SCO_Election_Campaign_On
			}
			random_list = {
				14 = {
					activate_decision = SCO_Election_AI_SNP_Campaign_in_Highlands
				}
				14 = {
					activate_decision = SCO_Election_AI_SNP_Campaign_in_Aberdeenshire
				}
				14 = {
					activate_decision = SCO_Election_AI_SNP_Campaign_in_Fife
				}

					activate_decision = SCO_Election_AI_SNP_Campaign_in_Lanark
				}
				14 = {
					activate_decision = SCO_Election_AI_SNP_Campaign_in_Dumfries
				}
				15 = {
					activate_decision = SCO_Election_AI_SNP_Campaign_in_Lothian
				}
				14 = {
					activate_decision = SCO_Election_AI_SNP_Campaign_Raise_Party_Turnout
				}
			}
		}


	}
}

country_event = { #Generals Meeting Start
	id = SCO.7011
	title = SCO.7011.t
	desc = SCO.7011.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_scottish_soldiers

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event SCO.7011" }

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #SNP Campaign
		name = SCO.7011.a
		hidden_effect = {
			activate_mission = SCO_Paranoia_Generals_Meeting
			set_country_flag = SCO_Generals_Meeting
			set_temp_variable = { alert_id = 101 }
			add_TNO_alert_unless_exists = yes			
			random_list = {
				90 = {
					set_country_flag = SCO_Paranoia_Generals_Meeting_Normal
				}
				10 = {
					set_country_flag = SCO_Paranoia_Generals_Meeting_Bad
					modifier = {
						factor = 4
						check_variable = {
							SCOparanoia > 5
						}

					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #parania crisis radom event
	id = SCO.7033
	title = SCO.7033.t
	desc = SCO.7033.desc
	picture = GFX_report_event_scottish_soldiers

	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event SCO.7033" }

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	option = {
		name = SCO.7033.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = SCO_Paranoia_Removed
				}
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						has_country_flag = SCO_Generals_Meeting
						has_country_flag = SCO_Military_Police_in_Edinburgh
						has_country_flag = SCO_Ships_in_FoF
						has_country_flag = SCO_Paranoia_Aberdeen_airport
						has_country_flag = SCO_Military_Clyde
						has_country_flag = SCO_Military_Lossiemouth
						has_country_flag = SCO_Paranoia_Highlands
					}
				}
			}

			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						SCOparanoia > 7
					}
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = SCO_Paranoia_Coup
					}
				}

				country_event = {
					id = SCO.7045
				}
			}

			else = {


				random_list = {
					16 = {
						country_event = {
							id = SCO.7011
						}
						modifier = {
							has_country_flag = SCO_Generals_Meeting
							factor = 0
						}
					}
					14 = {
						country_event = {
							id = SCO.7022
						}
						modifier = {
							has_country_flag = SCO_Military_Police_in_Edinburgh
							factor = 0
						}
					}
					14 = {
						country_event = {
							id = SCO.7034
							days = 1
						}
						modifier = {
							has_country_flag = SCO_Ships_in_FoF
							factor = 0
						}
					}
					14 = {
						country_event = {
							id = SCO.7074
						}
						modifier = {
							has_country_flag = SCO_Paranoia_Aberdeen_airport
							factor = 0
						}

					}
					14 = {
						country_event = {
							id = SCO.7077
						}
						modifier = {
							has_country_flag = SCO_Military_Clyde
							factor = 0
						}
					}
					14 = {
						country_event = {
							id = SCO.7080
						}
						modifier = {
							has_country_flag = SCO_Military_Lossiemouth
							factor = 0
						}
					}
					14 = {
						country_event = {
							id = SCO.7086
						}
						modifier = {
							has_country_flag = SCO_Paranoia_Highlands
							factor = 0
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
